#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int main(){
int t;
double s,y;
cin>>s>>t;
if(s<=3)y=10;
else if(s>3&&s<=10)y=10+2.0*(s-3);
else y=10+14+3*(s-10);
if(t)y+=t/5*2;
cout<<fixed<<setprecision(0)<<y;
return 0;
}

è¾“å…¥æ ¼å¼ï¼š
è¾“å…¥åœ¨ä¸€è¡Œä¸­ç»™å‡ºæ¯”èµ›æ—¶é—´Tï¼ˆåˆ†é’Ÿï¼‰ã€‚

è¾“å‡ºæ ¼å¼ï¼š
åœ¨ä¸€è¡Œä¸­è¾“å‡ºæ¯”èµ›çš„ç»“æœï¼šä¹Œé¾Ÿèµ¢è¾“å‡º@@ï¼Œå…”å­èµ¢è¾“å‡º^_^ï¼Œå¹³å±€åˆ™è¾“å‡º--ï¼›åè·Ÿ1ç©ºæ ¼ï¼Œå†è¾“å‡ºèƒœåˆ©è€…è·‘å®Œçš„è·ç¦»ã€‚

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int main(){
int t,gui=0,rab=0,flag=1,cn=0;
cin>>t;
for(int i=1;i<=t;i++){
    gui+=3;
    if(flag==1){
        rab+=9;
        if(i%10==0&&rab>gui)flag=0;}
    else{
        cn++;
        if(cn==30){flag=1;cn=0;}}
}
if(gui>rab)cout<<"@_@ "<<gui;
else if(gui<rab)cout<<"^_^ "<<rab;
else cout<<"-_- "<<rab;
return 0;
}

int main(){

    cin>>a;
    if(a%2)cn1++;
    if(a%2==0)cn2++;
}

æ®è¯´ä¸€ä¸ªäººçš„æ ‡å‡†ä½“é‡åº”è¯¥æ˜¯å…¶èº«é«˜ï¼ˆå•ä½ï¼šå˜ç±³ï¼‰å‡å»100ã€å†ä¹˜ä»¥0.9æ‰€å¾—åˆ°çš„å…¬æ–¤æ•°ã€‚çœŸå®ä½“é‡ä¸æ ‡å‡†ä½“é‡è¯¯å·®åœ¨10%ä»¥å†…éƒ½æ˜¯å®Œç¾èº«æï¼ˆå³ | çœŸå®ä½“é‡ âˆ’ æ ‡å‡†ä½“é‡ | < æ ‡å‡†ä½“é‡Ã—10%ï¼‰ã€‚å·²çŸ¥å¸‚æ–¤æ˜¯å…¬æ–¤çš„ä¸¤å€ã€‚ç°ç»™å®šä¸€ç¾¤äººçš„èº«é«˜å’Œå®é™…ä½“é‡ï¼Œè¯·ä½ å‘Šè¯‰ä»–ä»¬æ˜¯å¦å¤ªèƒ–æˆ–å¤ªç˜¦äº†ã€‚

è¾“å…¥æ ¼å¼ï¼š
è¾“å…¥ç¬¬ä¸€è¡Œç»™å‡ºä¸€ä¸ªæ­£æ•´æ•°Nï¼ˆâ‰¤ 20ï¼‰ã€‚éšåNè¡Œï¼Œæ¯è¡Œç»™å‡ºä¸¤ä¸ªæ•´æ•°ï¼Œåˆ†åˆ«æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªäººçš„èº«é«˜Hï¼ˆ120 < H < 200ï¼›å•ä½ï¼šå˜ç±³ï¼‰å’ŒçœŸå®ä½“é‡Wï¼ˆ50 < W â‰¤ 300ï¼›å•ä½ï¼šå¸‚æ–¤ï¼‰ï¼Œå…¶é—´ä»¥ç©ºæ ¼åˆ†éš”ã€‚

è¾“å‡ºæ ¼å¼ï¼š
ä¸ºæ¯ä¸ªäººè¾“å‡ºä¸€è¡Œç»“è®ºï¼šå¦‚æœæ˜¯å®Œç¾èº«æï¼Œè¾“å‡ºYou are wan mei!ï¼›å¦‚æœå¤ªèƒ–äº†ï¼Œè¾“å‡ºYou are tai pang le!ï¼›å¦åˆ™è¾“å‡ºYou are tai shou le!ã€‚

è¾“å…¥æ ·ä¾‹ï¼š

è¾“å‡ºæ ·ä¾‹ï¼š

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int main(){
    int n,h,w3;
    cin>>n;
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
        cin>>h>>w3;
        double w=w3;
        w/=2.0; 
        double w2;
        w2=(h-100)*0.9;
            if(fabs(w2-w)<w2*0.1)cout<<"You are wan mei!"<<endl;
            else{
            if(w2<w)cout<<"You are tai pang le!"<<endl;
            else cout<<"You are tai shou le!"<<endl;}
    }
return 0;
}

è¾“å‡ºç¬¬ä¸€è¡Œé¦–å…ˆç»™å‡ºè¾¾åˆ°æœ€ä½åˆ†æ•°çº¿çš„è€ƒç”Ÿäººæ•° Mï¼Œéšå M è¡Œï¼Œæ¯è¡ŒæŒ‰ç…§è¾“å…¥æ ¼å¼è¾“å‡ºä¸€ä½è€ƒç”Ÿçš„ä¿¡æ¯ï¼Œè€ƒç”ŸæŒ‰è¾“å…¥ä¸­è¯´æ˜çš„è§„åˆ™ä»é«˜åˆ°ä½æ’åºã€‚å½“æŸç±»è€ƒç”Ÿä¸­æœ‰å¤šäººæ€»åˆ†ç›¸åŒæ—¶ï¼ŒæŒ‰å…¶å¾·åˆ†é™åºæ’åˆ—ï¼›è‹¥å¾·åˆ†ä¹Ÿå¹¶åˆ—ï¼Œåˆ™æŒ‰å‡†è€ƒè¯å·çš„å‡åºè¾“å‡ºã€‚

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
struct student{
    int num,de,cai,sum,flag;
};
bool cmp(student a,student b){
    if(a.flag!=b.flag)return a.flag <b.flag ;
    else if(a.sum!=b.sum)return a.sum>b.sum ;
    else if(a.de!=b.de)return a.de>b.de ;
    else return a.num<b.num;
}
int main(){
    ios::sync_with_stdio(false);
    int n,l,h,cn=0;
    cin>>n>>l>>h;
    student x[n];
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
        cin>>x[i].num >>x[i].de >>x[i].cai ;
        if(x[i].cai>=l&&x[i].de>=l){
            cn++;
            x[i].sum=x[i].cai +x[i].de ;
            if(x[i].cai >=h&&x[i].de >=h)x[i].flag=1;
            else if(x[i].de>=h)x[i].flag=2;
            else if(x[i].de>=x[i].cai )x[i].flag=3;
            else x[i].flag=4;
        }
        else i--,n--;
    }
    sort(x,x+n,cmp);
    cout<<cn<<endl;
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
        cout<<x[i].num <<" "<<x[i].de<<" "<<x[i].cai<<endl;
    }
    return 0;
}

è¾“å…¥ä¸º3ä¸ªæ­£æ•´æ•°ï¼Œåˆ†åˆ«ä»£è¡¨ä¸‰è§’å½¢çš„3æ¡è¾¹aã€bã€cã€‚

è¾“å‡ºæ ¼å¼ï¼š
å¦‚æœè¾“å…¥çš„è¾¹èƒ½æ„æˆä¸€ä¸ªä¸‰è§’å½¢ï¼Œåˆ™åœ¨ä¸€è¡Œå†…ï¼ŒæŒ‰ç…§

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int main(){
    int a,b,c;
    cin>>a>>b>>c;
    double s,area,perimeter;
    s=(a+b+c)/2.0;
    area=sqrt(s*(s-a)*(s-b)*(s-c));
    perimeter=a+b+c;
    if(a-b<c&&b-c<a&&c-a<b){
        cout<<fixed<<setprecision(2)<<"area = "<<area<<"; perimeter = "<<perimeter;
    }else cout<<"These sides do not correspond to a valid triangle";
return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int b[10];
int main(){
int n,a,k,max=0;
cin>>n;
for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
    cin>>a;
do{
        k=a%10;
        b[k]++;
        if(b[k]>max)max=b[k];
        a/=10;        
    }while(a);
}
cout<<max<<":";
for(int i=0;i<10;i++)
if(b[i]==max)cout<<" "<<i;
return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int isprime(int n){
if(n==2)return 1;
else{
    for(int i=2;i<=sqrt(n);i++){
        if(n%i==0)return 0;
    }
}
return 1;    
}
int main(){
int n;
cin>>n;
for(int i=2;i<n;i++){
    if(isprime(i)&&isprime(n-i)){
        cout<<n<<" = "<<i<<" + "<<n-i;break;
    }
} 
 
return 0;
}

int main(){
    char input[1010];
    double flag=1,ans;    
    int flag2=1,cn=0,j;
      scanf("%s", &input);
    if(input[0]=='-')flag=1.5;
    for(j=0;input[j] !='\0';j++){
        if(input[j]=='2')cn++;
    }
    if((input[j-1]-48)%2==0){flag2=2;}
    if(flag==1.5)j--;
    ans=(double)cn/(double)j*flag*flag2*100;
    cout<<fixed<<setprecision(2)<<ans<<"%";
    //printf("%.2f%%",out);
    return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
struct node{        
    int add;
    int data;
    int next;
}link[100100];
int main(){
    int first,n,t;
    cin>>first>>n;
    while(n--){
        cin>>t;
        cin>>link[t].data;
        cin>>link[t].next;
        link[t].add=t;
    }
    vector<int>v; 
    while(first!=-1){
        v.push_back(first);//é¡ºåºå­˜å‚¨åœ°å€ 
        first=link[first].next;
    }
    int x=v.size();
    for(int i=0;i<x/2;i++){
        cout<<setw(5)<<setfill('0')<<v[x-1-i]<<" "<<link[v[x-1-i]].data<<" "<<setw(5)<<setfill('0')<<v[i]<<endl;
        cout<<setw(5)<<setfill('0')<<v[i]<<" "<<link[v[i]].data<<" ";
        if(i==x/2-1&&x%2==0)cout<<-1;
        else cout<<setw(5)<<setfill('0')<<v[x-2-i]<<endl;
    }
    if(x&1)cout<<setw(5)<<setfill('0')<<v[x/2]<<" "<<link[x/2].data<<" "<<-1;
    return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int a1[1010],a2[1010],b1[1010],b2[1010],c1[1010],c2[1010],d1[1010],d2[1010],e1[1010],e2[1010];
int main(){
int n,m;
cin>>n;
for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
        cin>>a1[i]>>a2[i];                                             
cin>>m;
for(int i=0;i<m;i++)
        cin>>b1[i]>>b2[i];
int cn1=0,cn2=0,k=0,cn3=0;
for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
    for(int j=0;j<m;j++){
        if(a2[i]==b2[j]){cn3++;}
         c1[k]=a1[i]*b1[j];c2[k]=a2[i]+b2[j];
        //if(c2[k]!=0){c1[k]+=a1[i]*b1[j];cn2++;}
        cn1++;k++;
    }        
}
for(int j=0;j<cn1-cn2;j++){
    for(int i=0;i<cn1-cn2-1;i++){
        if(c2[i]<c2[i+1]){
            int t=c2[i+1];
            c2[i+1]=c2[i];
            c2[i]=t;
            int tt=c1[i+1];
            c1[i+1]=c1[i];
            c1[i]=tt;}    
        }
}
k=0;
for(int i=0;i<cn1-cn2;i++){

    //else {
        e1[k]=c1[k];
        e2[k]=c2[k];
        
    if(c2[i]==c2[i+1]){
    e1[k]=c1[i]+c1[i+1];k++;
    }k++;
}
for(int i=0;i<cn1-cn2;i++){
    if(e1[i]!=0)cout<<e1[i]<<" "<<e2[i];
    if(i!=cn1-cn2-1&&e1[i]!=0)cout<<" ";
}
cout<<endl;
cn1=0,cn2=0,k=0;
for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
    for(int j=0;j<m;j++){
        if(a2[i]==b2[j]){d1[k]=a1[i]+b1[j];d2[k]=a2[i];cn2++;a1[i]=b1[j]=0;k++;}
        cn1++;
    }            
}
for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
        if(a1[i]!=0){d1[k]=a1[i];d2[k]=a2[i];k++;}
for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
        if(b1[i]!=0){d1[k]=b1[i];d2[k]=b2[i];k++;}
for(int j=0;j<cn1-cn2-1;j++){
    for(int i=0;i<cn1-1;i++){
        if(d2[i]<d2[i+1]){
            int t=d2[i+1];
            d2[i+1]=d2[i];
            d2[i]=t;
            int tt=d1[i+1];
            d1[i+1]=d1[i];
            d1[i]=tt;}    
        }
}
for(int i=0;i<k;i++){
    cout<<d1[i]<<" "<<d2[i];
    if(i!=k-1)cout<<" ";
}
return 0;
}

using namespace std;
struct tell{
    char name[10];
    int date; 
    char tel[20];
}t[10],tt;
int main(){
int n;
cin>>n;
for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
    cin>>t[i].name>>t[i].date>>t[i].tel;
}
for(int i=0;i<n-1;i++){
    for(int j=0;j<n-1;j++){
        if(t[j].date>t[j+1].date){
            tt=t[j+1];
            t[j+1]=t[j];
            t[j]=tt;
        }
    }
}
for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
    cout<<t[i].name<<" "<<t[i].date<<" "<<t[i].tel<<endl;    
}
return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int main(){
    stack <double> q;
    string a[100];
    int n=-1,flag=0;
    while(cin>>a[++n]);
    for(int i=n-1;i>=0;i--){
        if(isdigit(a[i][a[i].size()-1])){
            q.push(atof(a[i].c_str()));
        }else{
            if(q.size()<2){flag=1;break;}
            double x1=q.top();q.pop();
            double x2=q.top();q.pop();
            if(a[i][0]=='+')q.push(x1+x2);
            else if(a[i][0]=='-')q.push(x1-x2);
            else if(a[i][0]=='*')q.push(x1*x2);
            else if(a[i][0]=='/'){
                if(x2==0){flag=1;break;}
                q.push(x1/x2);}                
            }      
    } 
    if(q.size()!=1)flag=1;
    if(flag)cout<<"ERROR";
    else cout<<fixed<<setprecision(1)<<q.top();
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int main(){
    string s;
    char a[110],b[110];
    int cn=0,cn2=0,flag=1;
    while(cin>>s&&s!="."){
        for(int i=0;i<s.size();i++){
        if(s[i]=='('||s[i]=='['||s[i]=='{'||s[i]==')'||s[i]==']'||s[i]=='}')a[cn++]=s[i];
        else if(s[i]=='/'&&s[i+1]=='*')a[cn++]='<',i++;
        else if(s[i]=='*'&&s[i+1]=='/')a[cn++]='>',i++;
        }
    }
    map<char,char>q;
    q['(']=')';
    q['[']=']';
    q['{']='}';
    q['<']='>';
    for(int i=0;i<cn;i++){
        if(a[i]=='('||a[i]=='['|| a[i]=='{'||a[i]=='<')b[cn2++]=a[i];
        else if(cn2&&q[b[cn2-1]]==a[i])cn2--;
        else{
            flag=0;
            cout<<"NO"<<endl;
            if(!cn2){//å¦‚æœaæ ˆä¸ºç©ºï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆç¼ºå°‘ä¸ä¹‹å¯¹åº”çš„å·¦æ‹¬å·
                if(a[i]=='>')cout<<"?-*/";
                else cout<<"?-"<<a[i];
            }
            else{//å¦‚æœæ ˆé¡¶å…ƒç´ ä¸ä¹‹ä¸åŒ¹é…ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆç¼ºå°‘ä¸æ ˆé¡¶å…ƒç´ ç›¸åŒ¹é…çš„å³æ‹¬å·
                if(b[cn2-1]=='<')cout<<"/*-?";
                else cout<<b[cn2-1]<<"-?";
            }
            break;
        }
    }
    if(flag){
        if(!cn2)cout<<"YES";//å¤„ç†å®Œä¹‹åï¼Œå¦‚æœæ ˆä¸ºç©ºï¼Œåˆ™è¡¨ç¤ºå®Œå…¨åŒ¹é…
        else {//å¦‚æœæœ‰å‰©ä½™ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆå°±æ˜¯ç¼ºå°‘å³æ‹¬å·
            cout<<"NO"<<endl;
            if(b[cn2-1]=='<')cout<<"/*-?";
            else cout<<b[cn2-1]<<"-?";    
        }
    }    
return 0;
}

å·²çŸ¥ä¸¤ä¸ªéé™åºé“¾è¡¨åºåˆ—S1ä¸S2ï¼Œè®¾è®¡å‡½æ•°æ„é€ å‡ºS1ä¸S2åˆå¹¶åçš„æ–°çš„éé™åºé“¾è¡¨S3ã€‚

è¾“å…¥æ ¼å¼:

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int a[100000000];
int main(){
    long long n,m=0;
    while(cin>>n&&n!=-1){
        a[m]=n;
        m++;
    }
    while(cin>>n&&n!=-1){
        a[m]=n;
        m++;
    }
    sort(a,a+m);
    if(m==0){
        cout<<"NULL";
    }else{
        for(int i=0;i<m;i++){
            cout<<a[i];
            if(i!=m-1)cout<<" ";
        }
    }
    return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
string a[4]={"G","P","L","T"};
int b[4];
int main(){
    string c;
    cin>>c;
    int x=c.length();
    for(int i=0;i<=x;i++){
            if(c[i]=='g'||c[i]=='G')b[0]++;
            if(c[i]=='p'||c[i]=='P')b[1]++;
            if(c[i]=='l'||c[i]=='L')b[2]++;
            if(c[i]=='t'||c[i]=='T')b[3]++;
    }
    int max=0;
    for(int i=0;i<4;i++)
    if(max<b[i])max=b[i];
    
    for(int i=0;i<max;i++){
        for(int j=0;j<4;j++){
            if(b[j]){cout<<a[j];b[j]--;}
        }
    }
return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int a[10];
int main(){
int y,n,cn=0,i;
cin>>y>>n;
for(i=y;;i++){
    int k=i;
    if(k/1000==0)a[0]++;
    while(k){
        int j=k%10;
        a[j]++;
        k/=10;}        
    for(int x=0;x<=9;x++)
        if(a[x])cn++;
    if(cn==n)break;
    cn=0;
    memset(a,0,sizeof(a));
}
cout<<i-y<<" ";

int s=i;
if(i*10<10000&&i*10>=10)cout<<0;
i*=10;
if(i*10<10000&&i*10>=100)cout<<0;
i*=10;
if(i*10<10000&&i*10>=1000)cout<<0;
cout<<s;
return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int main(){
    int n,M,k,t;
    cin>>n>>M;
    map<int,double>m,m2;
    while(M--){
        cin>>k;
        for(int i=0;i<k;i++){
            cin>>t;
            if(t>=0)m[t]+=(1.0/k);
            else m2[t]+=(1.0/k);//mä¸ºç”·ï¼Œm2ä¸ºå¥³
        }
    }
    int a,b;
    double max1=0,max2=0;
    vector<int>v,v2;
    map<int,double>::iterator it;
    for(it=m.begin();it!=m.end();it++){//mä¸ºç”·
        if(max1<(it->second)){
            v.clear();
            max1=it->second;
            v.push_back(it->first);//ä¿å­˜ç¼–å· 
        }else if(max1==it->second){
            v.push_back(it->first);//ä¿å­˜ç¼–å·
        }
    }
    for(it=m2.begin();it!=m2.end();it++){//m2ä¸ºå¥³
        if(max2<(it->second)){
            v2.clear();
            max2=it->second;
            v2.push_back(it->first);//ä¿å­˜ç¼–å·
        }else if(max2==(it->second)){
            v2.push_back(it->first);//ä¿å­˜ç¼–å·
        }
    }
    cin>>a>>b;
    vector<int>::iterator it2;
    if(a<0){    
        it2=v.begin();
        if(*it2!=b){
            for(it2=v.begin();it2!=v.end();it2++)
                cout<<a<<" "<<*it2<<endl;
        }else cout<<a<<" "<<b<<endl;
        it2=v2.end()-1;//è´Ÿæ•°å€’åºè¾“å‡º 
        if(*it2!=a){
            for(it2=v2.end()-1;it2>=v2.begin();it2--)
                cout<<b<<" "<<*it2<<endl;
        }else return 0;
    }
    else{
        it2=v2.end()-1;
        if(*it2!=b){
            for(it2=v2.end()-1;it2>=v2.begin();it2--)
                cout<<a<<" "<<*it2<<endl;
        }else cout<<a<<" "<<b<<endl;
        it2=v.begin();
        if(*it2!=a){
            for(it2=v.begin();it2!=v.end();it2++)
                cout<<b<<" "<<*it2<<endl;
        }else return 0;
    }
    return 0; 
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int main(){
    int n;
    cin>>n;
    int k=1;
    for(int i=1;i<n;i++)
        k*=10;
    
    int j,m,s=1,sum=0;
    for(int i=k;i<10*k;i++){
            j=i;
            while(j){
                m=j%10;
                j/=10;
                    for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
                    s*=m;
                sum+=s;
                s=1;
            }
        if(sum==i)cout<<i<<endl;sum=0;
    }
    return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
string a;
int b[4];
int main(){
int k=0,m=1,sum=0;
cin>>a;
reverse(a.begin(),a.end());
for(int i=0;i<4;++i){
    for(int j=0+k;j<8+k;++j){
    sum+=(a[j]-48)*m;
    m*=2;    
    }
    k+=8;m=1;
    b[i]=sum;
    sum=0;
} 
for(int i=3;i>=0;--i){
cout<<b[i];
if(i!=0)cout<<".";    
}    
return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int a[110],c[110];
int main(){
int n;
char b;
cin>>n;
cin>>a[0]>>b>>c[0];
int fz=a[0],fm=c[0];
for(int i=1;i<n;i++){
    cin>>a[i]>>b>>c[i];
    if(a[i]==0)continue;
    fz=fz*c[i]+fm*a[i];
    fm=fm*c[i];
}
if(fz==0){
    cout<<0;
    return 0;
}
int x=fz,y=fm;
if(x<0&&y>0||x>0&&y<0)cout<<'-';
fz=fabs(fz);
fm=fabs(fm);
int max=fz>fm?fz:fm;
for(int i=max;i>0;i--){
    if(fz%i==0&&fm%i==0){
        fz/=i;fm/=i;
        if(fz>=fm){
            cout<<fz/fm;
            if(fz%fm){
                cout<<" ";
                if(x<0&&y>0||x>0&&y<0)cout<<'-';
                cout<<fz%fm<<"/"<<fm;
            }
        }
        else cout<<fz<<"/"<<fm;
        break;
    }
}
return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int a[1010];
int main(){
int n,k,m,max=0;
cin>>n;
for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
    cin>>k;
    for(int j=0;j<k;j++){
    cin>>m;
    a[m]++;    
    if(a[m]>=max)max=a[m];
    }
}
for(int i=1000;i>=0;i--)
    if(a[i]==max){cout<<i<<" "<<max;break;}
return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int duei[110],school[100010];
int main(){
    int n,code=1;
    cin>>n;
    vector<vector<int> >v(n+1);//vectorçš„å¸¸ç”¨æ„é€ å‡½æ•°
    for(int i=1;i<=n;i++)
        cin>>duei[i];
    while(1){
        int flag=true;//ç»“æŸå¾ªç¯æ¡ä»¶ï¼Œåº§ä½éƒ½å®‰æ’å¥½ 
        for(int i=1;i<v.size();i++){//å„ä¸ªå­¦æ ¡ä¹‹é—´éå†
            if(v[i].size()<duei[i]*10){//åˆ¤æ–­è¯¥æ ¡å­¦ç”Ÿæ˜¯å¦éƒ½æœ‰åº§ä½ 
                flag=false; 
                if(school[code-1]!=i){//åˆ¤æ–­è¯¥åº§ä½ä¹‹å‰å­¦ç”Ÿæ˜¯å¦ä¸ºæœ¬æ ¡ 
                    v[i].push_back(code);//å­¦ç”Ÿå…¥åº§ 
                    school[code]=i;//æ ‡è®°è¯¥åº§ä½    
                    code++;     
                }else{
                    v[i].push_back(code+1);//å­¦ç”Ÿå…¥åº§ 
                    school[code+1]=i;//æ ‡è®°è¯¥åº§ä½
                    code+=2;
                }
            }     
        }
        if(flag)break;
    }
     for(int i=1;i<v.size();i++){
        cout<<"#"<<i<<endl;
        for(int j=0;j<v[i].size();j++){
            if(j!=0&&j%10)cout<<" ";
            if(j!=0&&!(j%10))cout<<endl;
            cout<<v[i][j];
        }cout<<endl;
    }
    return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
string a[10010];
int b[10010],c[10010];
int main(){
int n,sum=0;
cin>>n;
for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
    cin>>a[i]>>b[i];
    sum+=b[i];
}
int ave=sum/n/2,win=fabs(ave-b[0]);
for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
    c[i]=fabs(ave-b[i]);
    if(c[i]<win)win=c[i];
}
for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
    if(win==c[i]){cout<<ave<<" "<<a[i];}
}
return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int d[3];
int main(){
    int n,cn=0,m;
    cin>>n;
    do{
    cn++;
    d[0]=n/100;
    d[1]=(n/10)%10;
    d[2]=n%10;
    for(int j=0;j<2;j++){
        for(int i=0;i<2;i++){
            if(d[i]>d[i+1]){int temp=d[i];d[i]=d[i+1];d[i+1]=temp;}        
    }   }
        int min,max;
        min=100*d[0]+10*d[1]+d[2];
        max=d[0]+10*d[1]+100*d[2];
        m=max-min;
    cout<<cn<<':'<<" "<<max<<" "<<'-'<<" "<<min<<" "<<'='<<" "<<m<<endl;
        n=m;
    }while(n!=495);        
return 0;
}

7-49 æ±‚æ•´æ•°åºåˆ—ä¸­å‡ºç°æ¬¡æ•°æœ€å¤šçš„æ•° (15åˆ†)

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int a[1100],b[1100],c[1100];
int main(){
long long int i,n,max=0,maxn;
cin>>i;
for(int j=0;j<i;j++){
    cin>>b[j];
    a[j]=b[j];
}
for(int j=0;j<i;j++){
    for(int k=0;k<i;k++){
        if(a[j]==b[k])c[j]++;        
    }
    if(max<c[j]){
    maxn=j;
    max=c[j];}    
}
cout<<a[maxn]<<" "<<max;    
return 0;    
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int s[1010];
int main(){
int n,cn=0,k;
cin>>n;
for(int i=1;i<=n;i++){
    cin>>s[i];
    k=s[i];
    int flag=1;
    for(int j=1;j<=cn;j++){
        if(s[j]+s[i]<=100){
            flag=0;
            s[j]+=s[i];s[i]=0;
            cout<<k<<" "<<j<<endl;
            break;
            
        }
    }
    if(flag){
        cn++;
        int temp=s[cn];
        s[cn]=s[i];
        s[i]=temp;
        cout<<k<<" "<<cn<<endl;    
    }
}
cout<<cn;
return 0;     
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
char a[1010],b[1010];
int oj(char a[]){
    int x=strlen(a),sum=0;
    if(x>4)return 0;//å»ä½æ•°è¶…1000 
    else if(a[0]=='-')return 0;//å»è´Ÿæ•° 
    for(int i=0;i<x;i++){
        if(*(a+i)>='1'&&*(a+i)<='9')sum=10*sum+*(a+i)-'0';
        else return 0;//å»å°æ•°ï¼Œéæ³•å­—ç¬¦ 
    }
    if(sum>1000||sum<0)return 0;//æ•°å­—ä¸åœ¨[1,1000]å†… 
    return sum;//è¾“å‡ºæ­£æ•´æ•° 
}
int main(){
    int flag=1;
    scanf("%s%s",a,b);
    if(oj(a))cout<<oj(a)<<" + ";
    else cout<<"? + ",flag=0;
    if(oj(b))cout<<oj(b)<<" = ";
    else cout<<"? = ",flag=0;
    if(flag)cout<<oj(a)+oj(b);
    else cout<<"?";
return 0;
}

int a[17]={7,9,10,5,8,4,2,1,6,3,7,9,10,5,8,4,2};

int main(){
int n,sum=0,flag=0,flag2=0;
cin>>n;
for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
    flag=0;
    for(int j=0;j<18;j++){
        cin>>input[j];
        if(!(input[j]>=48&&input[j]<=57)&&j<17){
        flag=1;
        flag2=1;
        }
        if(j!=17)sum+=(input[j]-'0')*a[j];        
    }
    if(b[sum%11]!=input[17]){flag=1;flag2=1;}
    sum=0;
    if(flag){
        cout<<input;
        flag=1;cout<<endl;}
}
if(flag2==0)cout<<"All passed";
return 0;
}

7-55 æœ€é•¿å¯¹ç§°å­ä¸² (25åˆ†)

å¯¹ç»™å®šçš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œæœ¬é¢˜è¦æ±‚ä½ è¾“å‡ºæœ€é•¿å¯¹ç§°å­ä¸²çš„é•¿åº¦ã€‚ä¾‹å¦‚ï¼Œç»™å®šIs PAT&TAP symmetric?ï¼Œæœ€é•¿å¯¹ç§°å­ä¸²ä¸ºs PAT&TAP sï¼Œäºæ˜¯ä½ åº”è¯¥è¾“å‡º11ã€‚

è¾“å…¥æ ¼å¼ï¼š
è¾“å…¥åœ¨ä¸€è¡Œä¸­ç»™å‡ºé•¿åº¦ä¸è¶…è¿‡1000çš„éç©ºå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ã€‚

è¾“å‡ºæ ¼å¼ï¼š
åœ¨ä¸€è¡Œä¸­è¾“å‡ºæœ€é•¿å¯¹ç§°å­ä¸²çš„é•¿åº¦ã€‚

è¾“å…¥æ ·ä¾‹ï¼š
Is PAT&TAP symmetric?
è¾“å‡ºæ ·ä¾‹ï¼š
11

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int f[1010][1010];
int main(){
string a;
getline(cin,a);
int x=a.size(),max=0,cn=0,cn2=0,max2=0,k;
for(int i=0;i<x;i++){
    for(int j=0;j<=i;j++){
        if(a[i+j]!=a[i-j])break;
        cn+=2;
    }
    if(cn>max)max=cn;
    cn=0;
}
max--;
for(int i=0;i<x;i++){
    for(int j=0;j<=i;j++){
        if(a[i+j+1]!=a[i-j])break;
        cn2+=2;
    }
    if(cn2>max2)max2=cn2;
    cn2=0;
}
max2;
k=(max>max2)?max:max2;

if(x<2)cout<<1;
else cout<<k;

return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
char s[1000];
int main(){
int x,i=0,cn=0;
cin>>x;
do{
    i*=10;
    i+=1;
    s[cn]=i/x+'0';
    i%=x;
    cn++;
}while(i!=0);
for(i=0;s[i]=='0';i++);
cout<<(s+i)<<" "<<cn;
return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int main(){
int n;
char a;
cin>>n>>a;
int k,sum=0,cn=0;
for(int i=1;;i++){
    cn++;
    k=2*i-1;
    sum+=k;
    if((n+1)/2==sum){break;}
    if((n+1)/2<=sum){cn--;sum-=k;k=k-2;break;}
}
int j=0;
for(int i=cn;i>0;i--){
    int j1=j,k1=k;
    while(j1--)cout<<" ";
    while(k1--)cout<<a;
    cout<<endl;
    j++;
    k-=2;
}
    k=3,j=j-2;
for(int i=cn-1;i>0;i--){
    int j1=j,k1=k;
    while(j1--)cout<<" ";
    while(k1--)cout<<a;
    cout<<endl;
    j--;
    k+=2;
}
cout<<n-(2*sum-1);
return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
string str,A,B;
int main(){
int cn=0;
while(cin>>str){
    cn++;
    if(cn==2)A=str;
    if(cn==14)B=str;
}
if(cn-1<2)cout<<"Momo... No one is for you ...";
else if(cn-1<14)cout<<A<<" is the only one for you...";
else cout<<A<<" and "<<B<<" are inviting you to dinner...";
return 0;     
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
char b[1010][1010];
int main(){
int n,m;//nè¡Œmåˆ— 
cin>>n;
getchar();
string a;
getline(cin,a);
int k=a.length();
m=k/n;
if(k>n*m)m++;
int j=0;
for(int y=m;y>0;y--){
    int x=1;
    while(x<=n){
    if(j>=k){
    b[x++][y]=' ';continue;}    
    b[x++][y]=a[j++];
    
    }
}        
for(int j=1;j<=n;j++){
    for(int i=1;i<=m;i++){
        cout<<b[j][i];    
        }if(j!=n)cout<<endl;
    }
return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
char a[100100];
char b[27]={'0','z','y','x','w','v','u','t','s','r','q','p','o','n','m','l','k','j','i','h','g','f','e','d','c','b','a'};
int main(){
    int l,n;
    cin>>l>>n;
    int t=n,i=0;
    int s,w=0;
    while(t){
        s=t%26;
        t/=26;
        a[i]=b[s+w];
        w=1;
        a[i+1]=b[s+w];
        i++;
    }
    if(n%26==0){
        int k2,k3;    
            for(int k2=26;k2<=n;k2*=26){
                cout<<"a";
            }    
    return 0;
    }
    int k=l-i;
    while(k--)cout<<"z";
    for(int j=i-1;j>=0;j--){
        cout<<a[j];
    }

    return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
char a[110][110];
int main(){
int n,flag=1;
char b;
cin>>b>>n;
getchar();
        for(int j=0;j<n;j++){
            cin.getline(a[j],110);
        }
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
        for(int j=0;j<n;j++){
            if(a[i][j]!=a[n-i-1][n-j-1])flag=0;
        }    
    }
    if(flag)cout<<"bu yong dao le"<<endl;        
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
        for(int j=0;j<n;j++){
            if(a[n-i-1][n-j-1]!=' ')cout<<b;
            else cout<<' ';
        }
    cout<<endl;
    }    
return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int oj(int a){
    for(int i=2;i<=sqrt(a);i++){
        if(a%i==0)return 0;
    }
    return 1;
}
int main(){
    int n,cn=0;
    cin>>n;
    for(int i=2;i<=n-2;i++){
        if(oj(i)&&oj(i+2)){cn++;} 
    } 
    cout<<cn;
return 0;
}

7-65 èºæ—‹æ–¹é˜µ (20åˆ†)
æ‰€è°“â€œèºæ—‹æ–¹é˜µâ€ï¼Œæ˜¯æŒ‡å¯¹ä»»æ„ç»™å®šçš„Nï¼Œå°†1åˆ°NÃ—Nçš„æ•°å­—ä»å·¦ä¸Šè§’ç¬¬1ä¸ªæ ¼å­å¼€å§‹ï¼ŒæŒ‰é¡ºæ—¶é’ˆèºæ—‹æ–¹å‘é¡ºåºå¡«å…¥NÃ—Nçš„æ–¹é˜µé‡Œã€‚æœ¬é¢˜è¦æ±‚æ„é€ è¿™æ ·çš„èºæ—‹æ–¹é˜µã€‚

è¾“å…¥æ ¼å¼ï¼š
è¾“å…¥åœ¨ä¸€è¡Œä¸­ç»™å‡ºä¸€ä¸ªæ­£æ•´æ•°Nï¼ˆ<10ï¼‰ã€‚

è¾“å‡ºæ ¼å¼ï¼š
è¾“å‡ºNÃ—Nçš„èºæ—‹æ–¹é˜µã€‚æ¯è¡ŒNä¸ªæ•°å­—ï¼Œæ¯ä¸ªæ•°å­—å 3ä½ã€‚

è¾“å…¥æ ·ä¾‹ï¼š

è¾“å‡ºæ ·ä¾‹ï¼š
1 2 3 4 5
16 17 18 19 6

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int a[10][10]; 
int main(){
int n,x,y,cn;
x=y=cn=1;
cin>>n;
a[1][1]=1;
while(cn<n*n){
    while(y<n&&!a[x][y+1])a[x][++y]=++cn;
    while(x<n&&!a[x+1][y])a[++x][y]=++cn;
    while(y>1&&!a[x][y-1])a[x][--y]=++cn;
    while(x>1&&!a[x-1][y])a[--x][y]=++cn;
}
for(int i=1;i<=n;i++){
    for(int j=1;j<=n;j++){
        cout<<setw(3)<<a[i][j];
    }
    cout<<endl;
}
return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using  namespace std;
const int NUMBER=10e6;
int a[NUMBER];
int main(){
    int n,m,k;
    cin>>n;
    while(n--){
        cin>>m;
        if(m==1)continue;
        while(m--){
            cin>>k;
            a[k]++;
        }
    } 
    int j,h,flag=0;
    cin>>j;
    while(j--){
        cin>>h;
        if(!a[h]){
            if(flag)cout<<" ";
            cout.fill('0');
            cout<<setw(5)<<h;
            flag=a[h]=1;
        }
    }
    if(!flag)cout<<"No one is handsome";
    return 0;
}

#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int fa[30300],cn[30300];
int find(int x){//åå¤æ‰¾çˆ¶äº²ç»“ç‚¹ï¼Œç›´åˆ°æ‰¾åˆ°æ ¹èŠ‚ç‚¹
//    if(x=fa[x])return x;//
//    else return fa[x]=find(fa[x]);
    int a=x;
    while(x!=fa[x]) 
        x=fa[x];
    while(a!=fa[a]){//è·¯å¾„å‹ç¼© 
        int z=a;
        a=fa[a];
        fa[z]=x;
    }
    return x;
} 
int main(){
    ios::sync_with_stdio(false); 
    cin.tie(0);cout.tie(0);
    int n,m,k,a,b;
    cin>>n>>m;
    for(int i=1;i<=n;i++){//åˆå§‹åŒ– 
        fa[i]=i;
        cn[i]=1; 
    }
    while(m--){
        cin>>k>>a;
        for(int i=1;i<k;i++){// 
            cin>>b;
            int faA=find(a);//æŸ¥æ‰¾açš„æ ¹èŠ‚ç‚¹ 
            int faB=find(b);//æŸ¥æ‰¾bçš„æ ¹èŠ‚ç‚¹ 
            if(faA!=faB)fa[faA]=faB,cn[faB]+=cn[faA];//å¦‚æœä¸å±äºåŒä¸€é›†åˆï¼Œåˆå¹¶ //
        }
    }
    int max2=0; 
    for(int i=1;i<n;i++){
        max2=max(max2,cn[i]);
    }
    cout<<max2;
return 0;
}

è¾“å‡ºæ ¼å¼:
åœ¨Nè¡Œä¸­è¾“å‡ºæŒ‰è¦æ±‚æ’åºåçš„ç»“æœï¼Œå³ï¼šå½“C=1æ—¶ï¼ŒæŒ‰å­¦å·é€’å¢æ’åºï¼›å½“C=2æ—¶ï¼ŒæŒ‰å§“åçš„éé€’å‡å­—å…¸åºæ’åºï¼›å½“C=3æ—¶ï¼ŒæŒ‰æˆç»©çš„éé€’å‡æ’åºã€‚å½“è‹¥å¹²å­¦ç”Ÿå…·æœ‰ç›¸åŒå§“åæˆ–è€…ç›¸åŒæˆç»©æ—¶ï¼Œåˆ™æŒ‰ä»–ä»¬çš„å­¦å·é€’å¢æ’åºã€‚

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
struct student{
    int code,score;
    string name;
}stu[100100];

int n,c;
bool cmp(student a,student b){
    if(c==1) return a.code<b.code;
    else if(c==2) {
        if(a.name==b.name)return a.code <b.code ;
        return a.name<b.name;
    }
    else {
        if(a.score==b.score)return a.code <b.code ;
        return a.score<b.score;
    } 
}
int main(){
    cin>>n>>c;
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
        cin>>stu[i].code>>stu[i].name>>stu[i].score;
    sort(stu,stu+n,cmp);        
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
        cout<<setw(6)<<setfill('0')<<stu[i].code<<" "<<stu[i].name<<" "<<stu[i].score<<endl;         
    return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int k1[1001000],k2[1001000],v1[1001000],v2[1001000];
int main(){
    int n,m,a,b,cn=0,cn2=0,cn3=0,cn4=0,sum=0;
    cin>>n;
    while(n--){
        cin>>a;
        if(a<0)k1[cn++]=a;
        else k2[cn2++]=a;
    }
    cin>>m;
    while(m--){
        cin>>b;
        if(b<0)v1[cn3++]=b;
        else v2[cn4++]=b;
    }
    sort(k1,k1+cn);//è´Ÿæ•°ä»å°åˆ°å¤§æ’åº 
    sort(k2,k2+cn2,greater<int>());//æ­£æ•°ä»å¤§åˆ°å°æ’åº
    sort(v1,v1+cn3,less<int>());//è´Ÿæ•°ä»å°åˆ°å¤§æ’åº 
    sort(v2,v2+cn4,greater<int>());//æ­£æ•°ä»å¤§åˆ°å°æ’åº
    a=min(cn,cn3);
    b=min(cn2,cn4);
    for(int i=0;i<a;i++)
        sum+=k1[i]*v1[i];
    for(int i=0;i<b;i++)
        sum+=k2[i]*v2[i];    
    cout<<sum;        
    return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
struct number{
    int code,money=0,cn=0;
}num[10100];
bool cmp(number a,number b){
    if(a.money==b.money&&a.cn==b.cn)return a.code<b.code;
    else if(a.money==b.money)return a.cn>b.cn;
    else return a.money>b.money;
}
int main(){
    int n,k,a,b;
    cin>>n; 
    for(int i=1;i<=n;i++){
        num[i].code=i;
        cin>>k;
        while(k--){
            cin>>a>>b;
            num[a].money+=b;
            num[i].money-=b;
            num[a].cn++;
        }
    }
    sort(num+1,num+n+1,cmp);
    for(int i=1;i<=n;i++){
        cout<<num[i].code<<" "<<fixed<<setprecision(2)<<num[i].money*0.01<<endl;
    }
    return 0;
}

ä¹¦å·ï¼ˆ[1, 1000]å†…çš„æ•´æ•°ï¼‰ é”®å€¼ï¼ˆSæˆ–Eï¼‰ å‘ç”Ÿæ—¶é—´ï¼ˆhh:mmï¼Œå…¶ä¸­hhæ˜¯[0,23]å†…çš„æ•´æ•°ï¼Œmmæ˜¯[0, 59]å†…æ•´æ•°ï¼‰

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int isborr[1010],startime[1010];
int main(){
    int id,h,m,cn=0,sum=0,n;
    char type,temp;
    cin>>n;
    for(int day=0;day<n;){
        cin>>id>>type>>h>>temp>>m;
        if(!id){
            if(!cn)cout<<"0 0"<<endl;
            else cout<<cn<<" "<<fixed<<setprecision(0)<<1.0*sum/cn<<endl;
            day++;
            cn=sum=0;
            memset(isborr,0,sizeof(isborr));
        }else if(type=='S'){
            isborr[id]=1;
            startime[id]=h*60+m;
        }else if(type=='E'&&isborr[id]==1){
            isborr[id]=0;
            sum+=h*60+m-startime[id];
            cn++;
        }
    }
return 0;    
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int main(){
    string qus,ans;
    int n;
    cin>>n;
    getchar();
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
        getline(cin,qus);
        cout<<qus<<endl;
        cout<<"AI: "; 
        ans=qus;
        int z=ans.length();
        int cn=0;
        for(int j=0;j<z;j++){//åˆ é™¤é¦–ç©ºæ ¼ 
            if(ans[j]!=' ')cn++;
            while(ans[j]==' '&&cn==0)ans.erase(j,1);
            if(ans[j]!='I')ans[j]=tolower(ans[j]);//å¤§å†™è½¬å°å†™ 
        }cn=0;
        for(int j=z-1;j>=0;j--){//åˆ é™¤å°¾ç©ºæ ¼ 
            if(ans[j]!=' ')cn++;
            while(ans[j]==' '&&cn==0)ans.erase(j,1),z--;    
        }
        for(int j=0;j<z-1;j++){//åˆ é™¤ä¸­ç©ºæ ¼ 
            if(ans[j]==' '&&ans[j+1]==' ')ans.erase(j,1),j--,z--;
            if(ans[j]==' '&&(ans[j+1]<48||ans[j+1]>57&&ans[j+1]<65))ans.erase(j,1),z--;
        }
        for(int j=1;j<z;j++){//ç½®æ¢you me 
            if(ans[j]=='I'&&ans[j+1]<97&&ans[j-1]<97)ans.replace(j,1,"you"); 
            if(ans[j]=='m'&&ans[j+1]=='e'&&ans[j+2]<97&&ans[j-1]<97)ans.replace(ans.find("me"),2,"you");
        }
           for(int k=0;k<10;k++){//ç½®æ¢could you
               if(ans.find("could you")!=string::npos){
                   int it=ans.find("could you");
                   if(it==0&&ans[it+9]<65){
                       ans.replace(ans.find("could you"),9,"I could");
                   }
                if(it!=0&&ans[it-1]<65&&ans[it+9]<65){
                       ans.replace(ans.find("could you"),9,"I could");
               } 
           }
        }
           for(int k=0;k<10;k++){//ç½®æ¢ can you        
            if(ans.find("can you")!=string::npos){
                int it=ans.find("can you");
                if(it==0&&ans[it+7]<65){
                    ans.replace(ans.find("can you"),7,"I can");
                }
                if(it!=0&&ans[it-1]<65&&ans[it+7]<65){
                    ans.replace(ans.find("can you"),7,"I can");
                }
            }
        }
        if(ans.find("?")!=string::npos)ans.replace(ans.find("?"),1,"!");
        cout<<ans;//è¾“å‡º
        if(i!=n-1)cout<<endl;        
        }
    return 0;    
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int isprime(int n){ 
    if(n<=1)return 1;
    int sqr=(int)sqrt(1.0*n);
    for(int i=2;i<=sqr;i++){ 
        if(n%i==0)return 1;
    } 
    return 2;
} 
struct node{ 
    int num,degree;
};
vector<node>ans;
map<int,int>m2;
int main(){ 
    int l,r;
    cin>>l>>r;
    for(int i=r;i>=l;i--){ 
        int t=i,sum=t,tt=t,cn=0;
        vector<int>v[10010];
        map<int,int>m;//æ¯ä¸ªå¹³æ–¹å’Œï¼ŒåŠå…¶å‡ºç°æ¬¡æ•° 
        while(sum!=1){//è‹¥å¹²æ¬¡è¿­ä»£å¾—åˆ° 1
            t=sum;
            sum=0;
            while(t){//åšä¸€æ¬¡å¹³æ–¹å’Œ
            int    k=t%10;
                sum+=k*k;
                t/=10; 
            }    
            cn++;//ç‹¬ç«‹æ€§å°±æ˜¯ä¾é™„äºå®ƒçš„çš„å¹¸ç¦æ•°çš„ä¸ªæ•°
            m[sum]++;
            if(m[sum]==2)break;
        } 
        if(sum==1){ //æ£€éªŒå¹¸ç¦æ•°
            if(m2[tt]==1)continue;//æ£€éªŒç‹¬ç«‹æ€§
            ans.push_back({tt,cn*isprime(tt)});
            for(map<int,int>::iterator it=m.begin();it!=m.end();it++){
                m2[it->first]=it->second;
            }
        } 
    }     
    int z=ans.size();
    if(!z)cout<<"SAD"; 
    else{ 
        for(int i=z-1;i>=0;i--){ 
            cout<<ans[i].num<<" "<<ans[i].degree<<endl;
        } 
    }
    return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int main(){
int n;
char a,b,c;
cin>>n;
for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
    for(int j=0;j<4;j++){
        cin>>a>>b>>c;
        if(c=='T'){
            if(a=='A')cout<<1;
            else if(a=='B')cout<<2;
            else if(a=='C')cout<<3;
            else cout<<4;
        } 
    }
}        
return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
struct mooncake{
    double store,sell,price;
}cake[1010]; 
bool cmp(mooncake a,mooncake b){
    return a.price>b.price; 
}
int main(){
    int n;
    double d;
    cin>>n>>d; 
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
        cin>>cake[i].store;
    }
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
        cin>>cake[i].sell;
        cake[i].price =cake[i].sell/cake[i].store;
    }
    sort(cake,cake+n,cmp);
    double ans;
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
        if(cake[i].store<=d){
            d-=cake[i].store;
            ans+=cake[i].sell;
        }else{
            ans+=cake[i].price*d;
            break;
        }
    }
    cout<<fixed<<setprecision(2)<<ans;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
vector<int>v[100100];//10^5çš„é—¨åæ‰€é€šå‘çš„é—¨ 
int d[100100];//è¯¥ç‚¹çš„åº¦ï¼ˆ10^5çš„é—¨ï¼‰
void bfs(int i){//å¹¿æœæ¨¡æ¿ 
    queue<int>q;//1.å®šä¹‰é˜Ÿåˆ—qå¹¶å°†èµ·ç‚¹å…¥é˜Ÿ    
    q.push(i); 
    int j;
    while(q.size()){//2.ä¸€ä¸ªwhileå¾ªç¯ï¼Œæ¡ä»¶ä¸ºqéç©º 
        j=q.front();//3.å…ˆå–å‡ºé˜Ÿé¦–å…ƒç´ topï¼Œç„¶åè®¿é—®å®ƒ ï¼Œè®¿é—®åå°†å…¶å‡ºé˜Ÿ 
        q.pop();
        for(int k=0;k<v[j].size();k++){//4.å°†topçš„ä¸‹ä¸€å±‚èŠ‚ç‚¹ä¸­æœªæ›¾å…¥é˜Ÿçš„èŠ‚ç‚¹å…¥é˜Ÿ 
        q.push(v[j][k]);
        } 
    }
    cout<<j;
}
int main(){
    int n,k,t;
    cin>>n;
    for(int i=1;i<=n;i++){
        cin>>k;
        while(k--){
            cin>>t;
            d[t]++;//(éƒ½æœ‰çˆ¶ç»“ç‚¹)
            v[i].push_back(t);
        }
    }
    for(int i=1;i<=n;i++){//æ‰¾åº¦ä¸º0çš„ç‚¹ä½œä¸ºå…¥å£ 
        if(!d[i]){k=i;break;}
    }
    bfs(k);
    return 0;
}

7-83 å®¶åº­æˆ¿äº§ (25åˆ†)

ç»™å®šæ¯ä¸ªäººçš„å®¶åº­æˆå‘˜å’Œå…¶è‡ªå·±åä¸‹çš„æˆ¿äº§ï¼Œè¯·ä½ ç»Ÿè®¡å‡ºæ¯ä¸ªå®¶åº­çš„äººå£æ•°ã€äººå‡æˆ¿äº§é¢ç§¯åŠæˆ¿äº§å¥—æ•°ã€‚

è¾“å…¥æ ¼å¼ï¼š
è¾“å…¥ç¬¬ä¸€è¡Œç»™å‡ºä¸€ä¸ªæ­£æ•´æ•°Nï¼ˆâ‰¤1000ï¼‰ï¼ŒéšåNè¡Œï¼Œæ¯è¡ŒæŒ‰ä¸‹åˆ—æ ¼å¼ç»™å‡ºä¸€ä¸ªäººçš„æˆ¿äº§ï¼š

é¦–å…ˆåœ¨ç¬¬ä¸€è¡Œè¾“å‡ºå®¶åº­ä¸ªæ•°ï¼ˆæ‰€æœ‰æœ‰äº²å±å…³ç³»çš„äººéƒ½å±äºåŒä¸€ä¸ªå®¶åº­ï¼‰ã€‚éšåæŒ‰ä¸‹åˆ—æ ¼å¼è¾“å‡ºæ¯ä¸ªå®¶åº­çš„ä¿¡æ¯ï¼š

å®¶åº­æˆå‘˜çš„æœ€å°ç¼–å· å®¶åº­äººå£æ•° äººå‡æˆ¿äº§å¥—æ•° äººå‡æˆ¿äº§é¢ç§¯

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int fa[100100];
struct node{//ä¸ªäººä¿¡æ¯ 
    int id,house,area;
};
struct ans{//è¾“å‡ºç»“æœ 
    int id,cn;
    double ave_house,ave_area;
}; 
bool cmp(ans &a,ans &b){
    if(a.ave_area==b.ave_area)return a.id<b.id;
    else return a.ave_area>b.ave_area; 
}
void init(){
    for(int i=0;i<=100100;i++)
        fa[i]=i;
} 
int find(int x){
    if(x==fa[x])return x;
    else return fa[x]=find(fa[x]);
}
void merge(int a,int b){
    int faA=find(a);
    int faB=find(b);
    if(faA!=faB){
        fa[faA]=faB;
    }
}
int main(){
    ios::sync_with_stdio(false);
    cin.tie(0);cout.tie(0); 
    int n,id,p1,p2,k,id1,house,area;
    cin>>n;
    init();
    set<int>s1;//ä¿å­˜æ‰€æœ‰äººç¼–å· 
    map<int,node>m1;//ä¿å­˜å½“å‰ç¼–å·ï¼ŒåŸºæœ¬ä¿¡æ¯ 
    while(n--){ 
        cin>>id>>p1>>p2>>k;
        s1.insert(id);//
        if(p1!=-1){ 
            s1.insert(p1);//
            merge(id,p1);
        }  
        if(p2!=-1){ 
            s1.insert(p2);//
            merge(id,p2);
        } 
        while(k--){ 
            cin>>id1;
            s1.insert(id1);//
            merge(id,id1);
        } 
        cin>>house>>area;
        m1[id]=node{id,house,area};//
    } 
    set<int>s2;//æ‰€æœ‰å®¶åº­çš„æ ¹ç¼–å· 
    map<int,vector<int> >m2;//æ‰€æœ‰å®¶åº­æ ¹ç¼–å·ï¼Œå­ç¼–å·; 
    for(set<int>::iterator it=s1.begin();it!=s1.end();it++){//éå†æ‰€æœ‰ç¼–å· 
        int fa=find(*it); 
        m2[fa].push_back(*it);//æ¯ä¸ªç¼–å·å…¥å®ƒæ ¹ç»“ç‚¹çš„mapå€¼ 
        s2.insert(fa);//è®°å½•æ ¹ç»“ç‚¹ 
    } 
    cout<<s2.size()<<endl;
    vector<ans>v;//ä¿å­˜æ‰€æœ‰ç»“æœï¼Œæ–¹ä¾¿æ’åº 
    for(map<int,vector<int> >::iterator it=m2.begin();it!=m2.end();it++){ 
        int z=it->second.size();
        double sum1=0,sum2=0; 
        for(int i=0;i<z;i++){ 
            int t=it->second[i];
            sum1+=m1[t].house;
            sum2+=m1[t].area;
        } 
        v.push_back(ans{it->second[0],z,sum1/z,sum2/z});
    }    
    sort(v.begin(),v.end(),cmp);
    int z=v.size();
    for(int i=0;i<z;i++){
        cout<<setw(4)<<setfill('0')<<v[i].id<<" "<<v[i].cn<<" "<<fixed<<setprecision(3)<<v[i].ave_house<<" "<<v[i].ave_area<<endl;
    }
    return 0;
}

7-84 æ±‚åˆ†æ•°åºåˆ—å‰Né¡¹å’Œ (15åˆ†)

æœ¬é¢˜è¦æ±‚ç¼–å†™ç¨‹åºï¼Œè®¡ç®—åºåˆ— 2/1+3/2+5/3+8/5+â€¦ çš„å‰Né¡¹ä¹‹å’Œã€‚æ³¨æ„è¯¥åºåˆ—ä»ç¬¬2é¡¹èµ·ï¼Œæ¯ä¸€é¡¹çš„åˆ†å­æ˜¯å‰ä¸€é¡¹åˆ†å­ä¸åˆ†æ¯çš„å’Œï¼Œåˆ†æ¯æ˜¯å‰ä¸€é¡¹çš„åˆ†å­ã€‚

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int fz(int n);
int fm(int n);
int fm(int n){
    if(n==1)return 1;
    else return fz(n-1);
 
}
int fz(int n){
    if(n==1)return 2;
    else return fz(n-1)+fm(n-1);
}
int main(){
    int n;
    cin>>n;
    double sum=0;
    for(int j=n;j>0;j--)
    sum+=(double)fz(j)/(double)fm(j);
    cout<<fixed<<setprecision(2)<<sum;
    return 0;
}

#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int t[1000100];
map<int,int>m;
int main(){
    int n,M,cn=0,flag=0;
    cin>>n;
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
        cin>>t[i];
        m[t[i]]++;
    }    
    cin>>M;
    cout<<n-m[M]<<endl;
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
        if(t[i]!=M){
        if(flag++)cout<<" ";
        cout<<t[i];    
        }
    return 0;
}
